        select distinct codclien  from Mconsultas where fecha_cita between '05/19/2016' and '05/19/2016'and asistido=3   and codmedico= s.codmedico 
    )
    
    ) AS decimal )/COUNT( distinct P.codclien )  efectividad
    from Mconsultas P
    inner join Mmedicos m On m.Codmedico=P.codmedico
    where P.fecha_cita between '05/19/2016' and '05/19/2016' and asistido=3 
    GROUP BY P.codmedico order by efectividad desc

        select distinct codclien  from Mconsultas where fecha_cita between '05/19/2016' and '05/19/2016'and asistido=3   and codmedico= s.codmedico 
    )
    
    )  compras ,
    max( concat(m.nombre+' ',m.apellido)) medico,
    CAST ((
    select COUNT( distinct s.codclien ) compras  from view_percentstats s where s.fechafac between '05/19/2016' and '05/19/2016' and s.codmedico=P.codmedico
     AND s.codclien in (
        select distinct codclien  from Mconsultas where fecha_cita between '05/19/2016' and '05/19/2016'and asistido=3   and codmedico= s.codmedico 
    )
    
    ) AS decimal )/COUNT( distinct P.codclien )  efectividad
    from Mconsultas P
    inner join Mmedicos m On m.Codmedico=P.codmedico
    where P.fecha_cita between '05/19/2016' and '05/19/2016' and asistido=3

    select COUNT( distinct s.codclien ) compras  from view_percentstats s where s.fechafac between '01/01/2015' and '12/31/2015' and s.codmedico=P.codmedico
     AND s.codclien in (
        select distinct codclien  from Mconsultas where fecha_cita between '01/01/2015' and '12/31/2015'and asistido=3   and codmedico= s.codmedico 
    )
    
    ) AS decimal )/COUNT( distinct P.codclien )  efectividad
    from Mconsultas P
    inner join Mmedicos m On m.Codmedico=P.codmedico
    where P.fecha_cita between '01/01/2015' and '12/31/2015' and asistido=3 
    GROUP BY P.codmedico order by efectividad desc

        ,a.codcompany
        ,a.codmedico 
        ,S.asistido
        ,a.id
        FROM view_audit a 
        inner join MClientes C ON C.codclien= a.codclien 
        inner join Mmedicos M ON M.Codmedico=a.codmedico 
        left join Mconsultas S ON S.codclien=a.codclien and S.fecha_cita=a.fechafac
        WHERE a.fechafac between '05/19/2018' and '05/19/2018' ORDER BY medico DESC,record OFFSET 0 ROWS FETCH NEXT 25  ROWS ONLY
